lexeme: Kusettaja

###  Kusettaja₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Kusettaja* (scammer)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  10
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
